POSITION_MANAGEMENT_ADMIN_TempAssignmentOfMatrixRelationshipText:"Use this option to enable the synchronisation for vacant matrix positions.<\/br><\/br>When the setting is enabled:<\/br><\/br>-If an employee is unassigned from a position that is referenced by matrix relationships of other positions and there is another employee assigned to the same position,<\/br>then the job relationships of the employees assigned to the positions referring to employee who is unassigned from the position are transferred to another employee who is assigned to the same position.<\/br>-If an employee is unassigned from a position that is referenced by matrix relationships of other positions and there is no other employee assigned to the same position,<\/br>then the job relationships of the employees assigned the position referring to the employee who is unassigned from the position are transferred to the next available higher-level employee of the matrix position.<\/br>-When a position is updated with a new matrix relationship or a matrix relationship is changed which means that the related position is changed, and the related position is vacant, the following happens. The job relationships of the respective type of the employees assigned to the position are updated with the employee assigned to the higher-level position of the related position.<\/br>-The options for transferring job relationship aren\u2019t shown on the Termination and Internal Hire screens for the previous position. Instead, the transfer of job relationships happens automatically, as described previously.<\/br>-When a position is updated with a new matrix relationship or a matrix relationship is changed, which means that the related position is changed, and the related position is vacant, the following happens. The job relationships of the respective type of the employees assigned to the position are updated with the employee assigned to the higher level position of the related position.<\/br><\/br>When the setting is disabled, the matrix synchronisation works as follows:<\/br><\/br>-If an employee is unassigned from a position that is referenced by matrix relationships of other positions and there is an employee assigned to the same position,<\/br>then the job relationships of the employees assigned to the positions referring to the employee who was unassigned from the position are transferred to another employee of the same position.<\/br>-If an employee is unassigned from a position that is referenced by matrix relationships of other positions and there is no other employee assigned to the same position,<\/br>then the job relationships of the employees of the positions referring to the employee who left the position are removed.<\/br>-When an employee is assigned to a position that has matrix relationships but the matrix position is vacant, the job relationship for this employee is not added or updated.<\/br>-The Termination and Internal Hire screens show different options for transferring job relationships and the behaviour previously described does not apply to the position being vacated.<\/br>-When a position is updated with a new matrix relationship or a matrix relationship is changed, which means that the related position is changed, and the related position is vacant, the following happens.
